20:718:54315:26:26:89:92:572:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
20:719:54315:26:13:89:525:546:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:In  the  model,  we  included  indicators  as  to  whether  the  living  standard  of  the  household  
20:720:54418:13:14:89:526:533:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:has  increased  (LIVEUP)  or  decreased  (LIVEDOWN)  during  the  last  three  years.21  The  
20:721:54512:14:14:89:529:519:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:estimated  coefficient  of  the  variable  LIVEUP  is  not  statistically  significant,  which  
20:722:54608:14:14:89:528:505:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:implies  that  increased  household  living  standards  do  not  affect  choices  relating  to  
20:723:54704:14:14:89:526:491:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children’s  engagement  in  work  activities.  However,  the  coefficient  of  the  LIVEDOWN  
20:724:54798:14:13:89:526:477:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:variable  was  statistically  significant  for  alternatives  1  and  3.  This  result  indicates  that  if  
20:725:54907:13:14:89:526:464:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:household  living  standards  decrease,  children  are  6.9  percentage  points  less  likely  to  be  
20:726:55010:14:14:89:528:450:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:not  working  or  involved  in  chores,  but  at  the  same  time  the  probability  of  children  
20:727:55109:14:26:89:479:436:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:combining chores and extra-household work increases by 6.4 percentage points.  
20:728:55188:26:14:89:92:410:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
20:729:55188:14:13:89:526:396:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Evidence  to  date  suggests  that  the  Vietnamese  trade  liberalisation  process  has  increased  
20:730:55289:13:14:89:525:383:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:overall household incomes and has not led to a decline in living standards for the poor in 
20:731:55380:14:14:89:529:369:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:general    (Thonburn  and  Jones,  2002).  Nevertheless,  it  is  still  expected  that  trade  
20:732:55476:14:14:89:526:355:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:liberalisation will create some winners and losers. For the winners, we hypothesised that 
20:733:55566:14:14:89:527:341:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:a  decline  in  child  labour  would  be  more  likely.  However,  the  results  from  the  Young  
20:734:55665:14:13:89:528:327:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Lives  dataset  indicate  that  the  incidence  of  child  labour  has  not  declined  as  living  
20:735:55764:13:14:89:525:314:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:standards have improved. It should be remembered, though, that our results refer only to 
20:736:55853:14:14:89:527:300:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:a  cohort  of  eight-year-old  children,  and  broader  generalisations  should  be  made  with  
20:737:55950:14:14:89:526:286:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:caution.. For the losers, our results indicate that decreased living standards increased the 
20:738:56043:14:14:89:526:272:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:probability  of  children’s  greater  involvement  in  work  activities.  This  is  worrying  as  a  
20:739:56144:14:13:89:526:258:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:growing  international  body  of  literature  suggests  that  children  deprived  of  educational  
20:740:56243:13:14:89:527:245:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:opportunities  are  more  likely  to  remain  poor  into  adulthood  and  in  turn  pass  on  their  
20:741:56344:14:14:89:525:231:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:poverty status to their children, in a process termed the intergenerational transmission of 
20:742:56436:14:14:89:254:217:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:poverty (eg, Harper et al., 2003).  
20:743:56472:14:14:89:92:203:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
20:744:56472:14:13:89:525:189:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Finally,  we  turn  our  discussion  to  community-level  variables.  We  hypothesised  that  the  
20:745:56571:13:14:89:525:176:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:accessibility of school measured by physical distance to school (SCHDIS3) and financial 
20:746:56659:14:14:89:527:162:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:expenses  (PRIMACOST)  would  increase  the  probability  of  a  child  working.  However,  
20:747:56751:14:14:89:527:148:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the  estimated  coefficient  of  this  variable  was  not  statistically  significant.  This  may  be  
20:748:56854:14:14:89:527:134:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:largely  attributed  to  the  fact  that  only  1.2  per  cent  of  the  sample  children  had  never  
20:749:56957:14:13:89:528:120:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:attended  school  and  just  3.3  per  cent  did  not  attend  school  the  previous  year.  The  
20:750:57055:13:14:89:525:107:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:proportion of poor households per community had a statistically significant effect on the 
20:751:57145:14:14:89:527:93:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:probability  of  a  child  doing  domestic  chores  but  decreased  the  probability  of  a  child  
20:752:57245:14:0:89:527:79:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:working  outside  the  household.  The  reason  may  be  that  children  in  poorer  communes  
21:753:57342:0:13:89:525:708:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:may have fewer employment opportunities, and thus the only way they can contribute to 
21:754:57428:13:14:89:424:695:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the household livelihood is through involvement in domestic chores.  
21:755:57497:14:14:89:92:681:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
21:756:57497:14:14:89:526:667:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:We  also  hypothesised  that  the  presence  of  a  factory  close  to  the  commune  may  induce  
21:757:57596:14:14:89:525:653:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children  into  work  (either  in  the  factory  or  in  related  supporting  units),  but  this  variable  
21:758:57704:14:25:89:270:639:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:emerged as statistically insignificant. 
21:759:57744:25:14:89:525:614:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:There are also regional differences with respect to the patterning of child work. Children 
21:760:57835:14:14:89:525:600:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:from Phu Yen and Ben Tre provinces are less likely to be involved in domestic work only 
21:761:57923:14:14:89:524:586:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:(j=2) and more likely to get involved in work both outside and inside the household (j=3). 
21:762:58014:14:14:89:527:572:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Children  from  Lao  Cai  and  Hung  Yen  provinces  are  less  likely  to  sit  idle  than  their  
21:763:58114:14:13:89:525:558:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:counterparts and more likely to get involved in chores and external work (see Alternative 
21:764:58204:13:14:89:233:545:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:3 in Table 5.3, Appendix C).  
21:765:58234:14:14:89:92:531:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
21:766:58234:14:14:89:161:517:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:5.5 Summary 
21:767:58246:14:14:89:92:503:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
21:768:58246:14:13:89:528:489:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:In  our  analysis  using  Young  Lives  data,  we  did  not  find  a  significant  statistical  
21:769:58342:13:14:89:528:476:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:relationship  between  improving  household  prosperity  and  a  reduction  in  child  work  
21:770:58435:14:14:89:529:462:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:activities.  This  suggests  that  a  threshold  effect  may  be  in  operation  and  that  the  
21:771:58532:14:14:89:526:448:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:improvements  in  household  living  standards  recorded  by  Young  Lives  households  may  
21:772:58625:14:14:89:527:434:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:not  have  been  significant  enough  to  have  a  positive  spillover  impact  on  child  labour.  
21:773:58725:14:13:89:526:420:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Indeed the cross-regional research by Edmonds and Turk (2004) discussed above would 
21:774:58809:13:14:89:527:407:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:suggest  that  this  threshold  is  related  to  an  average  GDP  per  capita.  However,  falling  
21:775:58909:14:14:89:527:393:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:living  standards  increased  the  probability  of  children’s  engagement  in  domestic  and  
21:776:59004:14:14:89:525:379:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:extra-household work. This indicates that social impact analyses of post-WTO accession 
21:777:59091:14:14:89:526:365:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:in  Vietnam  should  pay  careful  attention  to  the  well-being  of  vulnerable  groups  whose  
21:778:59189:14:13:89:525:351:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:livelihoods are likely to be negatively affected by trade-induced shocks, in both the short 
21:779:59281:13:14:89:200:338:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and the medium term.  
21:780:59303:14:14:89:92:324:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
21:781:59303:14:14:89:527:310:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Whether  children’s  involvement  in  work  has  any  negative  spillover  impact  on  other  
21:782:59397:14:13:89:528:296:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:dimensions  of  their  well-being,  such  as  educational  attainment  and  health  status,  is  
21:783:59494:13:14:89:268:283:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f7:B:addressed in the following chapters.  
21:784:59532:14:0:89:92:269:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
22:785:59534:0:14:89:384:706:195:g_d0_f7:195:g_d0_f7:C:6. Children’s schooling and academic attainment 
22:786:59582:14:14:89:92:692:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
22:787:59582:14:13:89:175:678:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:6.1 Introduction 
22:788:59599:13:14:89:92:665:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
22:789:59599:14:14:89:527:651:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Education  is  an  important  investment  in  human  capital  and  endows  children  with  the  
22:790:59695:14:14:89:526:637:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:means  to  improve  their  skills,  knowledge,  health  and  future  real  incomes  (eg,  Becker,  
22:791:59794:14:13:89:524:623:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:1962). Human capital can be broadly defined as ‘an individual’s productive skills, talents, 
22:792:59886:13:14:89:525:610:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and knowledge’ (Thurow, 1970: 1) and people invest in human capital to benefit from it 
22:793:59973:14:14:89:527:596:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:in  both  monetary  and  non-monetary  terms.  Vietnam  has  a  long  tradition  of  respect  for  
22:794:60072:14:14:89:526:582:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:education  and  its  90  per  cent  literacy  rates  and  school  enrolment  levels  were  among  the  
22:795:60175:14:14:89:525:568:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:highest  in  Southeast  Asia  in  the  1980s  (Swinkels  and  Turk,  2003).  However,  during  the  
22:796:60275:14:13:89:526:554:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:mid-1990s,  school  enrolment  levels  declined,  and  there  were  high  drop-out  rates  in  the  
22:797:60375:13:14:89:525:541:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:final years of primary school.22 Some attribute this falling enrolment and rising drop-out 
22:798:60466:14:14:89:524:527:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:rates to economic reforms which resulted in a shrinking education budget and led to a rise 
22:799:60557:14:14:89:526:513:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:in  private  tuition  (Liu,  2001a;  Hong,  2000).  Vo  and  Trinh  (2004)  point  out  that  budget  
22:800:60659:14:14:89:526:499:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:constraints  are  hindering  improvements  in  the  quality  of  education  and  training  systems  
22:801:60759:14:13:89:525:485:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:in Vietnam. However, recently there has been significant improvement in drop-out rates, 
22:802:60847:13:14:89:525:472:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:which have decreased from 27.7 per cent in 1993 to 12.4 per cent in 2002 (Vo and Trinh, 
22:803:60935:14:14:89:126:458:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:2004).  
22:804:60943:14:14:89:92:444:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
22:805:60943:14:14:89:522:430:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:In this section we focus on educational achievement among the Young Lives eight-year-
22:806:61028:14:13:89:525:416:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:old cohort as there is negligible variance in enrolment rates in our sample.23 We look at 
22:807:61118:13:14:89:529:403:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:two  dimensions  of  achievement.  First,  we  examine  the  determinants  of  children’s  
22:808:61209:14:14:89:525:389:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:scholastic achievement as measured by simple reading, writing and numeracy skills tests. 
22:809:61298:14:14:89:526:375:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Second,  we  look  at  an  important  and  idiosyncratic  feature  of  the  Vietnamese  schooling  
22:810:61397:14:14:89:525:361:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:system – private tuition. Investing in private tuition is increasingly common even among 
22:811:61486:14:13:89:526:347:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:poor  households,  as  indicated  in  Table  6.1.  We  believe  that  this  is  a  useful  indicator  of  
22:812:61592:13:26:89:504:334:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:households’ willingness to invest in the human capital development of their children.  
22:813:61679:26:14:89:529:308:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:We  also  assume  that  the  impacts  of  trade  liberalisation  on  child  welfare  will  be  
22:814:61774:14:14:89:526:294:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:channelled  through  household-  and/or  community-level  variables.  If  trade  liberalisation  
22:815:61871:14:14:89:526:280:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:leads  to  income  growth  and  increased  fiscal  spending  on  educational  facilities,  then  we  
22:816:61972:14:13:89:527:266:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:expect  positive  impacts  on  child  well-being.  In  addition,  we  also  address  the  question  
22:817:62072:13:14:89:527:253:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:raised  in  the  previous  section  as  to  whether  child  labour  has  adverse  consequences  on  
22:818:62172:14:14:89:528:239:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:other  dimensions  of  children  well-being,  namely  educational  attainment  and  school  
22:819:62264:14:14:89:147:225:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:attendance. 
22:820:62276:14:20:89:92:211:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
22:821:62276:20:13:89:246:191:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:6.2 Theoretical considerations 
22:822:62307:13:14:89:92:178:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
22:823:62307:14:14:89:525:164:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Economic  literature  that  models  educational  achievement  is  embedded  in  human  capital  
22:824:62403:14:14:89:526:150:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:theory  and  the  household  production  model  first  introduced  by  Becker  (1962)  and  later  
22:825:62502:14:14:89:525:136:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:developed  further  by  Leibowitz  (1974),  Becker  and  Tomes  (1979,  1986)  and  Hanushek  
22:826:62596:14:13:89:525:122:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:(1979, 1986). The educational production function has become the main construct of the 
22:827:62683:13:14:89:526:109:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:empirical  literature  to  identify  the  relative  importance  of  measurable  educational  inputs.  
22:828:62785:14:0:89:524:95:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Analogous to factory production, this framework relates contemporaneous child cognitive 
23:829:62875:0:13:89:526:708:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:attainment  with  educational  inputs  from  within  the  family  and  school.  To  facilitate  our  
23:830:62976:13:14:89:405:695:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:discussion, Figure 6.1 represents these factors diagrammatically.  
23:831:63043:14:14:89:92:681:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
23:832:63043:14:14:89:526:667:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:In Becker’s (1962) human capital model, people with different family backgrounds have 
23:833:63129:14:14:89:525:653:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:different optimal levels of schooling. Family background is considered important because 
23:834:63218:14:13:89:526:639:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:parents  with  more  resources  are  more  able  to  invest  in  their  children.  But  the  question  
23:835:63321:13:14:89:525:626:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:remains, why do parents invest in their children? This question is addressed in the model 
23:836:63411:14:14:89:525:612:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:of intergenerational transmission of human capital (eg, Becker and Tomes, 1986). Parents 
23:837:63500:14:14:89:526:598:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:are  assumed  to  care  about  the  lifetime  utility/welfare  of  their  children  and  thus  seek  to  
23:838:63605:14:14:89:527:584:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:influence  their  children’s  human  capital.  If  they  have  sufficient  assets  or  can  borrow  
23:839:63705:14:13:89:526:570:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:funds  against  their  children’s  future  income,  they  invest  in  the  human  capital  of  each  
23:840:63806:13:14:89:525:557:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:child up to the point where the marginal rate of return on human capital equals the rate of 
23:841:63898:14:14:89:529:543:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:interest.  However,  because  human  capital  is  poor  collateral  (Becker,  1962)  in  an  
23:842:63991:14:14:89:525:529:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:imperfect capital market, parents cannot borrow as they would wish to finance investment 
23:843:64080:14:14:89:525:515:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:in the schooling of their children. As a result, human capital investment is constrained by 
23:844:64172:14:13:89:525:501:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:parents’ wealth or income and students from less wealthy families are more likely to drop 
23:845:64262:13:14:89:526:488:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:out  because  of  greater  financial  constraints.  In  addition,  conceptualising  the  family  as  a  
23:846:64366:14:14:89:525:474:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:production unit, this framework posits that a child’s educational attainment is also subject 
23:847:64459:14:14:89:508:460:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:to parental decisions on fertility and household willingness to invest in human capital.  
23:848:64549:14:14:89:92:446:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
23:849:64549:14:13:89:526:432:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Although investment in human capital models advanced by Becker (1962)[CHANGED]) 
23:850:64628:13:14:89:526:419:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and  Becker  and  Tomes  (1986)  yield  testable  hypotheses  with  respect  to  the  effects  of  
23:851:64727:14:14:89:525:405:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:family factors on the decision to invest in children and their scholastic achievement, these 
23:852:64819:14:14:89:525:391:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:models  offer  little  empirical  guidance.  In  this  vein,  Leibowitz’s  model  (1974)  of  human  
23:853:64920:14:14:89:525:377:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:capital production (see Figure 6.1) provides an operational way to investigate educational 
23:854:65011:14:13:89:525:363:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:achievement. In this model, parents’ genetic endowments are passed on to their children, 
23:855:65099:13:14:89:525:350:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and in turn partly determine children’s abilities. Parental education and ability influences 
23:856:65192:14:14:89:525:336:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:family income levels and the quality and quantity of both time and goods invested in their 
23:857:65283:14:14:89:526:322:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:offspring.  This  is  termed  ‘home  investment’.  This  model  is  silent,  however,  on  the  role  
23:858:65385:14:13:89:528:308:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:played  by  school-related  factors  in  producing  human  capital  and  thus  we  employ  a  
23:859:65479:13:14:89:528:295:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:modified  version  to  compensate  for  this  shortcoming.24  The  process  of  augmenting  
23:860:65571:14:14:89:525:281:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:human capital in students also takes place at school. Resources and teachers’ knowledge 
23:861:65659:14:14:89:525:267:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and skills are expected to be important in determining the process of augmenting human 
23:862:65746:14:14:89:528:253:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:capital  in  students.  As  illustrated  in  Figure  6.1,  school-related  factors  are  subject  to  
23:863:65848:14:14:89:520:239:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:parental choice of school, which is influenced by parental ability, education and income.  
23:864:65939:14:19:89:92:225:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:

25:976:68944:13:14:94:537:423:121:g_d0_f7:121:g_d0_f6:F:Total 993           100                      994           100                      1,000           100           
25:977:69058:14:14:89:92:409:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
25:978:69058:14:14:89:525:395:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:The choice of independent variables included in our models is shaped by the availability 
25:979:69147:14:13:89:527:381:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:of  data,  economic  theories  and  previous  studies.  Table  6.3  in  Appendix  D  provides  
25:980:69242:13:14:89:525:368:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:summary statistics of variables used in our regression. As before, we broadly group these 
25:981:69332:14:14:89:525:354:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:variables into three groups: (a) child characteristics; (b) household characteristics; and (c) 
25:982:69427:14:14:89:223:340:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:community-level variables. 
25:983:69454:14:14:89:92:326:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
25:984:69454:14:13:89:219:312:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:(a) Child characteristics  
25:985:69481:13:14:89:525:299:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:These are often used in the modelling of children’s educational attainment. They include 
25:986:69570:14:14:89:525:285:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:gender, age, ethnicity, and birth order. As we use the eight-year-old child dataset, we can 
25:987:69661:14:14:89:525:271:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:only control for gender, birth order and ethnicity and not for age differences. As the effect 
25:988:69755:14:14:89:525:257:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:of gender (MALE) on educational achievement is not unambiguous, it will be determined 
25:989:69841:14:13:89:526:243:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:in  the  empirical  analysis.  As  for  ethnicity  (KIDETHNIC),  the  data  reveals  that  children  
25:990:69942:13:14:89:525:230:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:from the Kinh ethnic group are more likely to receive private tuition than ethnic minority 
25:991:70033:14:14:89:526:216:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children (52 per cent versus 17.6 per cent). With respect to birth order (ORDER), being 
25:992:70121:14:14:89:527:202:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:an  early-born  child  suggests  that  one  would  have  a  better  chance  of  accessing  fuller  
25:993:70220:14:14:89:526:188:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:parental attention and household resources without sharing with later-born children. The 
25:994:70308:14:13:89:525:174:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:implication is that elder children would be more likely to attend extra classes and perform 
25:995:70400:13:14:89:198:161:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:better academically.    
25:996:70424:14:14:89:92:147:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
25:997:70424:14:14:89:247:133:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f6:B:(b) Household level variables   
25:998:70456:14:14:89:530:119:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:First,   we   use   a   wealth   index   (WEALTHINDEX)   to   proxy   for   family   income,   
25:999:70551:14:13:89:526:105:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:hypothesising  that  better-off  families  would  have  more  resources  to  afford  extra  classes  
25:1000:70652:13:14:89:526:92:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:for  their  children  (usually  these  extra  classes  are  run  by  schoolteachers),  and  be  able  to  
25:1001:70758:14:0:89:344:78:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:provide more support for their children’s education.  
26:1002:70814:0:13:89:92:708:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
26:1003:70814:13:14:89:525:695:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:We also include a number of covariates in the model to capture the economic background 
26:1004:70901:14:14:89:527:681:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:of  the  household.  They  include  whether  the  family  own  the  house  they  are  living  in  
26:1005:70999:14:14:89:527:667:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:(OWNHOUSE),  are  land  owners  (OWNLAND),  in  debt  (DEBT),  and  the  number  of  
26:1006:71084:14:14:89:525:653:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:rooms in the house (NUMROOM). As proxies for household prosperity, we expect these 
26:1007:71167:14:13:89:525:639:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:variables to be positively related to a child receiving private tuition and performing better 
26:1008:71261:13:14:89:163:626:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:scholastically.  
26:1009:71278:14:14:89:92:612:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
26:1010:71278:14:14:89:525:598:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Parental schooling may influence their decision about whether to invest in private tuition 
26:1011:71369:14:14:89:526:584:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and  to  support  their  child’s  education.  Better-educated  parents  may  be  more  willing  to  
26:1012:71469:14:13:89:526:570:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:spend  time  to  help  their  children  with  their  studies,  thus  children  born  to  more  highly  
26:1013:71572:13:14:89:525:557:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:educated parents are expected to be more likely to have a private tutor and to do better on 
26:1014:71664:14:14:89:176:543:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:basic skills tests.  
26:1015:71685:14:14:89:92:529:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
26:1016:71685:14:14:89:525:515:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:The number of siblings in the family may also affect school achievement. The underlying 
26:1017:71773:14:13:89:527:501:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:assumption  is  that  there  is  a  trade-off  between  child  quality  and  quantity  (Becker  and  
26:1018:71874:13:14:89:527:488:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Tome,  1979,  1986;  Behrman  and  Knowles  1999;  Hanushek,  1992).  In  our  empirical  
26:1019:71964:14:14:89:527:474:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:analysis  we  control  not  only  for  the  number  of  siblings  (NUMSIB)  but  also  for  the  
26:1020:72061:14:14:89:527:460:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:number  of  boys  (BOYBORN)  and  girls  born  (GRLBORN).  For  family  structure,  we  
26:1021:72149:14:14:89:527:446:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:include  an  indicator  for  female-headed  families  (FEMALEHEAD).  It  is  expected  that  
26:1022:72242:14:13:89:526:432:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children from female-headed households will be worse off than children in male-headed 
26:1023:72328:13:14:89:526:419:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:households  and  this  may  lower  their  chances  of  attending  private  tuition  classes  and  in  
26:1024:72430:14:14:89:268:405:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:turn performing well academically.   
26:1025:72467:14:14:89:92:391:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
26:1026:72467:14:14:89:527:377:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:As  negative  events  could  affect  household  livelihoods  and  in  turn  children’s  access  to  
26:1027:72567:14:13:89:531:363:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:extra   tuition,   we   include   indicators   of   families’   experience   of   negative   events   
26:1028:72669:13:14:89:529:350:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:(NEGATIVEEVENT).  We  hypothesise  that  negative  events  may  lower  chances  of  
26:1029:72753:14:14:89:525:336:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children receiving extra tuition and performing well academically. We also include in our 
26:1030:72842:14:14:89:525:322:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:model an indicator of negative events leading to a loss of income. We expect that this will 
26:1031:72934:14:13:89:527:308:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:lower  the  probability  of  parents  investing  in  private  tuition.  We  also  include  variables  
26:1032:73036:13:14:89:531:295:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:indicating  whether  household  living  standards  have  improved  (LIVEUP)  or  declined    
26:1033:73129:14:14:89:298:281:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:(LIVEDOWN) during the last three years.  
26:1034:73170:14:14:89:92:267:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
26:1035:73170:14:14:89:248:253:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f6:B:(c) Community characteristics 
26:1036:73199:14:13:89:527:239:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:The  following  community  and  macro-level  variables  are  used  in  our  model.  First,  we  
26:1037:73295:13:14:89:525:226:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:expect increased direct costs of education to result in some parents cutting investment in 
26:1038:73386:14:14:89:525:212:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:private tutors for their children. We include the information of cost of primary education 
26:1039:73477:14:14:89:526:198:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:(PRIMACOST) at the community level in our model. The proportion of poor families in 
26:1040:73560:14:14:89:526:184:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the  community  (POORFAM)  may  also  affect  the  probability  of  children  getting  extra  
26:1041:73654:14:13:89:526:170:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:tuition.  Distance  to  school  may  also  affect  child  education.  The  farther  the  school  from  
26:1042:73757:13:14:89:525:157:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the household the less likely we think children will be receiving extra classes. We control 
26:1043:73849:14:14:89:525:143:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:for distance to school in our analysis (SCHDIS3). We also include dummy variables for 
26:1044:73935:14:14:89:527:129:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:different  provinces  (PHUYEN,  BENTRE,  LAOCAI  and  HUNGYEN),  but  these  were  
26:1045:74018:14:14:89:528:115:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:automatically  dropped  by  the  STATA  statistical  package  we  employed,  suggesting  a  
26:1046:74110:14:13:89:230:101:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:problem of multi-colinarity.  
26:1047:74140:13:0:89:92:88:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
27:1048:74142:0:13:89:270:708:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:6.4 Discussion of estimation results 
27:1049:74179:13:14:89:92:695:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
27:1050:74179:14:14:89:237:681:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:6.4.1 Attending extra classes 
27:1051:74209:14:14:89:525:667:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Table 6.3 in Appendix D presents the estimation results for the model of receiving extra 
27:1052:74298:14:14:89:525:653:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:tuition. We estimated two specifications, one with the inclusion of indicators for a child’s 
27:1053:74391:14:13:89:528:639:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:involvement  in  labour  and  domestic  chores  and  one  without.  We  do  not  find  any  
27:1054:74483:13:14:89:526:626:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:significant  differences  between  boys  and  girls  nor  among  children  from  different  ethnic  
27:1055:74583:14:14:89:529:612:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:groups.  This  latter  finding  is  very  interesting  as  the  raw  data  indicates  a  marked  
27:1056:74680:14:14:89:526:598:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:difference  between  the  two  groups.  It  points  to  the  importance  of  controlling  for  family  
27:1057:74783:14:14:89:449:584:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:background variables when considering differences among ethnic groups.  
27:1058:74855:14:13:89:92:570:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
27:1059:74855:13:14:89:526:557:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Turning  to  the  household  level  variables,  the  results  are  striking.  The  most  significant  
27:1060:74957:14:14:89:527:543:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:variables  are  related  to  economic  status.  The  variable  WEALTHINDEX  is  statistically  
27:1061:75052:14:14:89:529:529:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:significant  with  a  large  magnitude.  This  indicates  that  household  prosperity  is  an  
27:1062:75147:14:14:89:526:515:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:important  determinant  of  parents  investing  in  children’s  educational  development.  This  
27:1063:75244:14:13:89:526:501:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:finding  is  consistent  with  findings  reported  by  Behrman  and  Knowles  (1999)  using  the  
27:1064:75342:13:14:89:352:488:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Vietnam Household Living Standard Survey 1992/93. 
27:1065:75392:14:14:89:92:474:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
27:1066:75392:14:14:89:525:460:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:The  variables  indicating  economic  shocks  (NEGATIVEEVENT  and  HHJOB),  however,  
27:1067:75478:14:14:89:525:446:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:were not statistically significant. Nor were they with the two variables indicating changes 
27:1068:75569:14:13:89:528:432:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:in  the  living  standards  of  the  family  over  the  previous  three  years  (LIVEUP  and  
27:1069:75663:13:14:89:527:419:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:LIVEDOWN).  Consistent  with  the  findings  on  child  labour,  this  result  suggests  that  
27:1070:75758:14:14:89:468:405:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:families seek to shield children from the negative effects of economic shocks.  
27:1071:75838:14:14:89:92:391:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
27:1072:75838:14:14:89:525:377:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:At the community level, the proportion of poor households per commune was statistically 
27:1073:75926:14:13:89:525:363:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:significant. This implies that in poor communes, the trend of investing in private tuition is 
27:1074:76020:13:14:89:526:350:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:weaker.  Other  variables  (distance  to  school  and  the  cost  of  primary  education)  were  not  
27:1075:76122:14:14:89:207:336:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:significant statistically.  
27:1076:76150:14:14:89:92:322:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
27:1077:76150:14:13:89:530:308:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Finally,   we   turn   to   variables   reflecting   children’s   labour   status   (CHORESONLY,   
27:1078:76249:13:14:89:526:295:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:WORKCHORE).  The  variable  CHORESONLY  is  negative  and  statistically  significant,  
27:1079:76337:14:14:89:527:281:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:indicating  that  the  more  a  child  is  involved  in  domestic  chores,  the  less  likely  she/he  
27:1080:76440:14:14:89:529:267:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:would  attend  private  tuition  classes.  However,  the  variable  WORKCHORE  is  not  
27:1081:76528:14:14:89:526:253:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:statistically significant, although it has the expected negative sign. In short, this suggests 
27:1082:76622:14:13:89:525:239:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:that if trade liberalisation results in an increase in child labour (both outside employment 
27:1083:76714:13:14:89:528:226:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and  domestic  work)  it  may  lower  children’s  longer-term  scholastic  performance  by  
27:1084:76806:14:14:89:334:212:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:lowering their chance of attending extra classes.27  
27:1085:76859:14:14:89:92:198:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
27:1086:76859:14:14:89:240:184:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:6.4.2 Educational attainment 
27:1087:76888:14:13:89:527:170:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Table  6.4  in  Appendix  D  presents  the  estimation  results  for  children’s  achievement  in  
27:1088:76987:13:14:89:525:157:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:basic academic skills tests. We estimated three specifications which differ with respect to 
27:1089:77078:14:14:89:526:143:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the  inclusion  of  three  variables,  EXTRACLASS,  WORKCHORE  and  CHORESONLY.  
27:1090:77159:14:14:89:526:129:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:We  first  discuss  the  results  of  specification  1.  With  respect  to  children’s  characteristics,  
27:1091:77265:14:14:89:423:115:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:there are no gender or ethnic differences on the numeracy skills test.  
27:1092:77337:14:0:89:92:101:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
28:1093:77339:0:13:89:529:708:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Turning  to  household  variables,  the  gender  of  the  household  head  and  birth  order  were    
28:1094:77441:13:14:89:526:695:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:not  statistically  significant.  Parental  schooling,  however,  was  found  to  have  a  positive  
28:1095:77542:14:14:89:529:681:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:impact  on  children’s  numeracy  skills,  although  maternal  education  alone  was  not  
28:1096:77633:14:14:89:526:667:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:statistically  significant.  In  terms  of  family  structure,  the  number  of  siblings  (NUMSIB)  
28:1097:77734:14:14:89:522:653:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:was negative but statistically insignificant, thus not supporting the quality–quantity trade-
28:1098:77827:14:13:89:528:639:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:off  hypothesis.  The  variables  indicating  a  decreased  living  standard  was  statistically  
28:1099:77925:13:14:89:525:626:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:significant although the variable indicating increased living standard was not. Perhaps the 
28:1100:78017:14:14:89:530:612:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:single   most   important   determinant   of   child’s   numerical   skill   attainment   was   the   
28:1101:78119:14:14:89:529:598:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:WEALTHINDEX  variable,  reaffirming  the  importance  of  economic  background  in  
28:1102:78203:14:14:89:525:584:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:shaping children’s educational achievement. Nevertheless, economic shocks did not have 
28:1103:78290:14:13:89:264:570:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:an impact on numeracy test scores.  
28:1104:78326:13:14:89:92:557:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
28:1105:78326:14:14:89:526:543:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:At  the  community  level,  distance  to  school,  the  proportion  of  poor  households  and  the  
28:1106:78426:14:14:89:470:529:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:average cost of education in the community were all statistically insignificant.  
28:1107:78508:14:14:89:92:515:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
28:1108:78508:14:13:89:525:501:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:We  now  turn  to  specification  2,  which  includes  an  indicator  for  attending  extra  classes.  
28:1109:78611:13:14:89:527:488:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:However,  perhaps  surprisingly,  additional  tuition  did  not  have  any  beneficial  effect  on  
28:1110:78711:14:14:89:225:474:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:numeracy skill acquisition.  
28:1111:78740:14:14:89:92:460:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
28:1112:78740:14:14:89:521:446:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Specification 3 includes two indicators for children’s involvement in domestic and extra-
28:1113:78829:14:13:89:526:432:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:household  work  activities.  However,  surprisingly  the  involvement  of  children  in  labour  
28:1114:78927:13:14:89:522:419:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and chores was correlated with superior numeracy skills. An explanation for this counter-
28:1115:79016:14:14:89:527:405:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:intuitive  finding  might  be  that  a  more  able  child  may  be  more  likely  to  be  asked  by  
28:1116:79117:14:14:89:527:391:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:his/her  parents  to  help  with  work  activities  and/or  be  more  likely  to  find  a  job.  The  
28:1117:79219:14:14:89:527:377:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:argument  here  would  be  that  a  self-selection  process  is  in  operation,  with  more  able  
28:1118:79318:14:13:89:526:363:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children  juggling  both  work  and  education.  Ideally,  we  should  model  this  self-selection  
28:1119:79418:13:14:89:525:350:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:process through a bivariate model or instrumentation. However, owing to data limitations 
28:1120:79507:14:14:89:530:336:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:we   were   unable   to   find   an   appropriate   instrument   for   the   CHORESONLY   and   
28:1121:79603:14:14:89:526:322:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:WORKCHORES  variables.  Although  the  results  should  be  interpreted  with  caution,  the  
28:1122:79697:14:13:89:527:308:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:conclusion  here  is  that  we  do  not  find  strong  evidence  that  child  labour  and  domestic  
28:1123:79798:13:14:89:480:295:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:chores have a negative impact on the development of children’s numeracy skills. 
28:1124:79878:14:14:89:92:281:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
28:1125:79878:14:14:89:526:267:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Tables 6.5 and 6.6 in Appendix D report estimated results from ordinal logit models for 
28:1126:79966:14:14:89:526:253:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children’s  writing  and  reading  skills,  respectively.  In  table  6.5  we  report  our  estimation  
28:1127:80070:14:13:89:528:239:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:results  for  three  specifications.  The  first  specification  does  not  include  indicators  for  
28:1128:80172:13:14:89:527:226:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children’s  involvement  in  private  tuition  classes,  work  and  chores.  According  to  the  
28:1129:80269:14:14:89:526:212:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:estimated results, there were no significant gender differences in writing skills, but Kinh 
28:1130:80361:14:14:89:528:198:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children  performed  better  than  ethnic  minority  children.  Later  birth  order  was  also  
28:1131:80457:14:14:89:525:184:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:correlated with superior writing skills, perhaps because these children are being helped by 
28:1132:80549:14:13:89:525:170:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:their older brothers or sisters. Parental schooling – both paternal and maternal – was also 
28:1133:80641:13:14:89:528:157:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:found  to  be  an  important  determinant  of  children’s  writing  abilities.  There  was  no  
28:1134:80737:14:14:89:526:143:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:evidence,  however,  of  a  trade-off  between  quantity  and  quality  –  that  is,  the  number  of  
28:1135:80840:14:14:89:526:129:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children  per  family  was  statistically  insignificant.  Nevertheless,  the  estimated  effects  of  
28:1136:80943:14:14:89:527:115:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the  number  of  boys  and  girls  born  within  the  household  are  negative  and  statistically  
28:1137:81043:14:0:89:526:101:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:significant.  In  terms  of  household  economics,  the  single  most  important  was  again  the  
29:1138:81144:0:13:89:527:708:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:WEALTHINDEX  variable.  However,  changes  in  household  living  standards,  although  
29:1139:81232:13:14:89:286:695:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:negative, were statistically insignificant. 
29:1140:81276:14:14:89:92:681:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
29:1141:81276:14:14:89:525:667:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:At the community level, proximity to school was positively correlated with better writing 
29:1142:81366:14:14:89:525:653:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:skills. Higher average costs of schooling also improved performance but we believe this 
29:1143:81454:14:13:89:525:639:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:is  likely  to  be  capturing  the  broader  economic  well-being  of  the  community  which  may  
29:1144:81553:13:14:89:531:626:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:be correlated with greater parental investment in their children’s educational development.  
29:1145:81646:14:14:89:92:612:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
29:1146:81646:14:14:89:527:598:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:In  specification  2,  we  included  a  variable  for  children’s  involvement  in  private  tuition  
29:1147:81748:14:14:89:525:584:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:classes. As expected, this variable was positive and statistically significant, indicating the 
29:1148:81843:14:13:89:524:570:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:beneficial effects of attending extra classes on children’s writing skills. In specification 3, 
29:1149:81939:13:14:89:525:557:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:we include two indicators for children’s extra-household work and chores status. As with 
29:1150:82028:14:14:89:530:543:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the   numeracy   skills   results,   the   work–chore   variable   was   statistically   significant,   
29:1151:82132:14:14:89:473:529:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:suggesting that able children are able to cope with work and school at this age.  
29:1152:82214:14:14:89:92:515:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
29:1153:82214:14:13:89:528:501:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:The  estimated  results  for  reading  skills  are  presented  in  Table  6.6.  Boys  and  girls  
29:1154:82312:13:14:89:528:488:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:performed equally well but Kinh children outperformed their ethnic minority counterparts. 
29:1155:82402:14:14:89:525:474:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Maternal education was found to be important in positively influencing children’s reading 
29:1156:82491:14:14:89:528:460:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:skills.  The  wealth  index  was  again  significant,  but  the  variable  indicating  perceived  
29:1157:82589:14:14:89:526:446:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:changes in household wealth were not.28 Negative events counter-intuitively emerged as 
29:1158:82675:14:13:89:525:432:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:positive and significant and we are unable to offer an explanation for this, but economic 
29:1159:82765:13:14:89:526:419:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:shocks  leading  to  loss  of  income  has  the  expected  negative  sign  and  was  statistically  
29:1160:82865:14:14:89:527:405:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:significant.  This  result  suggests  that  economic  shocks  may  have  a  negative  spillover  
29:1161:82962:14:14:89:247:391:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:impact on children’s education.  
29:1162:82995:14:14:89:92:377:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
29:1163:82995:14:13:89:526:363:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Turning to specification 2, once again, private tuition improved children’s reading skills. 
29:1164:83086:13:14:89:526:350:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:But in specification 3, no statistically significant correlation with child work was found, 
29:1165:83178:14:14:89:502:336:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:suggesting that at this age there is no negative impact on their basic reading abilities.  
29:1166:83269:14:14:89:92:322:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
29:1167:83269:14:13:89:161:308:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:6.5 Summary 
29:1168:83281:13:14:89:92:295:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
29:1169:83281:14:14:89:525:281:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:In general the estimated results are consistent with the empirical literature on educational 
29:1170:83374:14:14:89:528:267:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:attainment,  which  argues  that  individual  and  family  background  variables  constitute  
29:1171:83468:14:14:89:528:253:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:important  determinants  of  a  child’s  educational  attainment.  Importantly,  the  variable  
29:1172:83564:14:13:89:525:239:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:LIVEDOWN was found to have a negative impact on children’s educational attainment. 
29:1173:83647:13:14:89:526:226:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Thus,  if  trade  liberalisation  results  in  a  negative  downturn  for  some  households,  Young  
29:1174:83748:14:14:89:525:212:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Lives  findings  suggest  that  this  will  have  a  negative  impact  on  children’s  human  capital  
29:1175:83851:14:14:89:522:198:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:accumulation. Surprisingly, however, variables related to children’s involvement in extra-
29:1176:83941:14:14:89:522:184:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:household and domestic work activities were either not statistically significant for eight-
29:1177:84032:14:13:89:424:170:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:year-old children or, in the case of numeracy and writing, positive.29  
29:1178:84104:13:16:89:92:157:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
29:1179:84104:16:15:89:246:141:195:g_d0_f7:195:g_d0_f7:C:7. Children’s heath status 
29:1180:84131:15:13:89:92:126:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
29:1181:84131:13:14:89:175:113:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:7.1 Introduction 
29:1182:84148:14:0:89:92:99:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
30:1183:84150:0:13:89:527:708:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Trade  liberalisation  and  market  openness  are  expected  to  bring  about  improved  life  
30:1184:84245:13:14:89:528:695:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:quality  through  increased  income,  greater  employment  opportunities,  better  choice  of  
30:1185:84340:14:14:89:529:681:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:goods  and  services,  including  healthcare,  through  greater  market  opportunities  and  
30:1186:84433:14:14:89:525:667:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:competition. But trade liberalisation may also have painful consequences for some groups 
30:1187:84522:14:14:89:525:653:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:of  the  population.  On  the  one  hand,  greater  openness  to  the  international  economy  may  
30:1188:84622:14:13:89:526:639:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:lead  to  an  increase  in  public  demand  for  government  safety  nets,  and  children’s  health  
30:1189:84723:13:14:89:528:626:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:status may benefit from this if these government safety nets are targeted at health (Rodrik, 
30:1190:84816:14:14:89:525:612:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:1999). Higher economic growth might also increase the government’s tax revenue, which 
30:1191:84902:14:14:89:525:598:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:could facilitate an increase in spending on children’s health. On the other hand, however, 
30:1192:84993:14:14:89:528:584:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:trade  liberalisation  might  affect  children’s  health  by  influencing  the  degree  to  which  
30:1193:85092:14:13:89:525:570:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:governments are willing and able to fund public health. Before Doi Moi, district hospitals 
30:1194:85183:13:14:89:526:557:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and  commune-level  health  centres  provided  medical  services  and  essential  drugs  free  of  
30:1195:85282:14:14:89:528:543:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:charge.  However,  as  a  consequence  of  liberalisation  of  the  health  sector  (with  the  
30:1196:85378:14:14:89:525:529:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:emergence of private hospitals and clinics) and a decrease in government budget support, 
30:1197:85467:14:14:89:526:515:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the public health system deteriorated because of the exodus of thousands of doctors and 
30:1198:85555:14:13:89:525:501:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:health workers. By 1991, commune-level health centres were not working (Hong, 2000). 
30:1199:85640:13:14:89:525:488:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:According to the World Bank, ‘the shortage of funds to the health centre is so acute; it is 
30:1200:85732:14:14:89:525:474:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:unclear where the grassroots facilities are going to find the inputs to continue functioning 
30:1201:85825:14:14:89:525:460:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:in the future’ (cited in Hong, 2000).30 However, the situation has improved thanks to the 
30:1202:85915:14:14:89:526:446:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:sustained GDP growth rate at over seven per cent and the new State Budget Law which 
30:1203:85999:14:13:89:527:432:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:was  passed  in  2004.  According  to  Tran  (2005),  the  government  has  given  priority  to  
30:1204:86096:13:14:89:528:419:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:improving  the  rural  healthcare  system.  Official  statistics  show  that  Vietnam  spends  
30:1205:86191:14:14:89:525:405:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:around five to six per cent of GDP on health expenditure. The share of government health 
30:1206:86280:14:14:89:493:391:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:spending at the local level (provincial and below) has also increased (Adam, 2005). 
30:1207:86364:14:14:89:92:377:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
30:1208:86364:14:13:89:261:363:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:7.2 Model specification and data  
30:1209:86398:13:14:89:92:350:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
30:1210:86398:14:14:89:527:336:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Various  measures  of  children’s  health  status  have  been  used  in  the  literature  including  
30:1211:86499:14:14:89:526:322:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children’s  survival  rate  (Wagstaff  and  Nguyen,  2002)  or  anthropometry  (height  for  age  
30:1212:86597:14:13:89:525:308:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and weight for age). The Young Lives survey has a measure of acute illness (ie, incidence 
30:1213:86687:13:14:89:525:295:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:of illness in the last two weeks). To model the health of a child, which is unobserved, we 
30:1214:86778:14:14:89:527:281:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:adopt  a  latent  variable  framework,31  which  can  be  considered  as  consistent  with  the  
30:1215:86875:14:14:89:525:267:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:literature on health production function. A child’s health can be seen as a stock of human 
30:1216:86966:14:14:89:526:253:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:capital,  which  at  any  point  in  time  can  be  determined  by  initial  genetic  endowment  and  
30:1217:87068:14:13:89:527:239:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:subsequent  investment.  A  change  in  a  child’s  health  status  is  determined  through  a  
30:1218:87164:13:14:89:355:226:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:production function which converts inputs into health.  
30:1219:87220:14:14:89:92:212:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
30:1220:87220:14:14:89:526:198:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:We  also  include  children’s  work  status  variables  and  assess  their  interaction  effect  as  in  
30:1221:87325:14:14:89:525:184:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the previous section on education. Descriptive statistics of these variables are provided in 
30:1222:87418:14:14:89:216:170:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Table 7.1 in Appendix E.  
30:1223:87444:14:13:89:92:156:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
30:1224:87444:13:14:89:216:143:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:(a) Child characteristics 
30:1225:87470:14:14:89:525:129:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:In Vietnam there is some preference towards boys, thus we expect boys to be more likely 
30:1226:87558:14:14:89:526:115:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:to  receive  more  attention  and  investment  from  parents,  resulting  in  better  health  status.  
30:1227:87661:14:13:89:525:101:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Differences between ethnic groups are left for the empirical exercise, although we expect 
30:1228:87751:13:0:89:527:88:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Kinh  children  to  be  more  likely  to  have  better  health  status  because  of  having  greater  
31:1229:87855:0:13:89:522:708:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:access to resources and public health facilities. With respect to birth order, being a first-
31:1230:87948:13:14:89:527:695:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:born  child  would  mean  having  better  chances  of  accessing  full  parental  attention  and  
31:1231:88046:14:14:89:330:681:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:household resources without sharing with others.  
31:1232:88096:14:14:89:92:667:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
31:1233:88096:14:14:89:242:653:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:(b) Household-level variables 
31:1234:88126:14:13:89:525:639:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Literature on the determinants of health suggests that there is a strong correlation between 
31:1235:88219:13:14:89:525:626:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:income and health (eg,Deaton 2006). In our analysis, we expect family income to have a 
31:1236:88306:14:14:89:527:612:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:strong  influence  on  children’s  health.  Better-off  families  (proxied  by  the  Young  Lives  
31:1237:88405:14:14:89:527:598:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:wealth  index)  would  have  more  resources  to  invest  in  their  children,  in  terms  of  food,  
31:1238:88507:14:14:89:527:584:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:nutrition  intake  and  better  access  to  health  facilities.  As  in  previous  chapters,  we  also  
31:1239:88611:14:13:89:526:570:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:include  a  number  of  covariates  in  the  model  to  capture  a  household’s  economic  status,  
31:1240:88711:13:14:89:525:557:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:including whether the family owns the house they are living in, owns land, is in debt, and 
31:1241:88802:14:14:89:525:543:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the number of rooms in the house. We expect these variables to be positively related to a 
31:1242:88892:14:14:89:193:529:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:child’s health status.  
31:1243:88916:14:14:89:92:515:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
31:1244:88916:14:13:89:526:501:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Parental  education  is  also  included  in  the  model,  as  we  hypothesise  that  better-educated  
31:1245:89018:13:14:89:525:488:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:parents may be able to transform a given bundle of resources into higher levels of health 
31:1246:89108:14:14:89:179:474:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:for their children.  
31:1247:89129:14:14:89:92:460:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
31:1248:89129:14:14:89:526:446:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:In our empirical analysis we control for the number of siblings as well as the number of 
31:1249:89218:14:13:89:524:432:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:boys and girls per family. For family structure, we include an indicator for female-headed 
31:1250:89309:13:14:89:527:419:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:households.  Due  to  the  feminisation  of  poverty,  we  hypothesise  that  children’s  health  
31:1251:89407:14:14:89:531:405:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:status   in   female-headed   families   would   be   worse   than   children   in   male-headed   
31:1252:89506:14:14:89:525:391:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:households. Lastly, we also assume that the effects of trade liberalisation on child health 
31:1253:89598:14:14:89:528:377:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:will  be  mediated  by  changes  in  household-level  variables  and  we  include  variables  
31:1254:89692:14:13:89:331:363:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:reflecting changes in household economic status.  
31:1255:89742:13:14:89:92:350:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
31:1256:89742:14:14:89:247:336:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:(c) Community characteristics 
31:1257:89772:14:14:89:526:322:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:A number of community and macro-level variables are used in our model. They include 
31:1258:89855:14:13:89:528:308:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the  proportion  of  poor  families  per  commune,  the  number  of  pharmacies  within  the  
31:1259:89949:13:14:89:525:295:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:neighbourhood and distance to health facilities. As discussed above, market reforms have 
31:1260:90038:14:14:89:525:281:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:led to a depletion of public health facilities, particularly at the commune level. This may 
31:1261:90130:14:14:89:527:267:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:have  serious  consequences  for  local  inhabitants  and  children.  In  order  to  capture  the  
31:1262:90229:14:14:89:527:253:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:effects  of  access  to  health  facilities  we  create  a  series  of  dummy  variables:  access  to  
31:1263:90332:14:13:89:528:239:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:public  hospitals  (HELDIS1),  access  to  private  hospitals  (HELDIS2),  access  to  local  
31:1264:90426:13:14:89:527:226:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:community  health  centres  (HELDIS3),  access  to  government  dispensary  (HELDIS5),  
31:1265:90514:14:14:89:486:212:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:access to private dispensary (HELDIS6), and distance to drug stores (HELDIS8).  
31:1266:90594:14:14:89:92:198:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
31:1267:90594:14:14:89:527:184:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Child  labour  causes  widespread  concern  because  of  the  potential  damaging  effects  on  
31:1268:90690:14:13:89:525:170:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:health. However, there is a paucity of empirical literature on the effects of child labour on 
31:1269:90784:13:14:89:526:157:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:health (O’Donnell et al., 2003). As Edmonds (2005a) and O’Donnell et al. (2003) argue, 
31:1270:90871:14:14:89:525:143:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the majority of child labour takes the form of farm work or domestic chores, rather than 
31:1271:90960:14:14:89:527:129:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:involvement  in  hazardous  work.  However,  the  effect  of  child  labour  on  health  is  not  
31:1272:91058:14:14:89:525:115:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:unambiguous.  On  the  one  hand,  involvement  in  any  type  of  labour  implies  some  toll  on  
31:1273:91158:14:13:89:526:101:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:young  bodies,  eg,  contact  with  harmful  fertilisers  and  pesticides  in  agricultural  labour,  
31:1274:91260:13:0:89:526:88:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:which may have a negative impact on health. On the other hand, child work may ensure 
32:1275:91346:0:13:89:524:708:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:physical fitness and mitigate against a sedentary lifestyle. To explore the potential impact 
32:1276:91439:13:14:89:533:695:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:of    child    labour    on    health,    we    include    two    variables,    WORKCHORES    and    
32:1277:91540:14:14:89:245:681:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:CHORESONLY, in the model.  
32:1278:91567:14:14:89:92:667:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
32:1279:91567:14:14:89:270:653:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:7.3 Discussion of estimation results 
32:1280:91604:14:13:89:92:639:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
32:1281:91604:13:14:89:527:626:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Table  7.2  in  Appendix  E  presents  the  estimation  results  for  these  three  specifications.  
32:1282:91705:14:14:89:525:612:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Specification 1 serves as the base model, which does not include indicators for access to 
32:1283:91795:14:14:89:526:598:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:health  facilities  and  children’s  involvement  in  labour  and  domestic  chores.  The  results  
32:1284:91895:14:14:89:525:584:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:from these three models are quite similar. Kinh children are found to be more likely to be 
32:1285:91986:14:13:89:526:570:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:ill.32 Birth order and the number of siblings are found to be statistically insignificant, ie, 
32:1286:92081:13:14:89:525:557:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:having no influence on the probability of children falling ill. At the family level, parental 
32:1287:92175:14:14:89:525:543:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:education – especially maternal education – is found to be important for a child’s health, 
32:1288:92266:14:14:89:475:529:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:suggesting that the caring practices of better-educated parents may be superior.  
32:1289:92348:14:14:89:92:515:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
32:1290:92348:14:13:89:528:501:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:The  economic  status  of  the  household  was  proxied  by  the  number  of  rooms  in  the  
32:1291:92442:13:14:89:527:488:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:household,  whether  the  family  was  in  debt  or  had  been  exposed  to  a  negative  event.  
32:1292:92540:14:14:89:529:474:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:However,   only   the   number   of   rooms   was   found   to   be   a   statistically   significant   
32:1293:92644:14:14:89:525:460:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:determinant of a child’s health. The two variables capturing changes in household living 
32:1294:92733:14:14:89:492:446:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:standards over time were not statistically significant and nor was the wealth index.  
32:1295:92819:14:13:89:92:432:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
32:1296:92819:13:14:89:526:419:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:The estimation results indicate that a child’s involvement in labour and domestic chores 
32:1297:92908:14:14:89:528:405:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:does  not  increase  the  probability  of  falling  ill. Our  finding  is  consistent  with  that  of  
32:1298:93010:14:14:89:526:391:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:O’Donnell et al. (2003) who found little evidence of a contemporaneous impact of child 
32:1299:93096:14:14:89:167:377:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:work on health. 
32:1300:93112:14:13:89:92:363:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
32:1301:93112:13:14:89:526:350:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:In  the  model  we  include  a  number  of  variables  indicating  the  accessibility  to  a  range  to  
32:1302:93217:14:14:89:526:336:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:health  facilities  as  discussed  above.  As  shown  in  Table  7.2,  distance  to  a  public  health  
32:1303:93321:14:14:89:527:322:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:centre  emerged  as  statistically  significant,  suggesting  that  access  to  public  healthcare  
32:1304:93421:14:13:89:527:308:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:plays  an  important  role  in  children’s  health.  This  is  also  consistent  with  findings  by  
32:1305:93522:13:14:89:525:295:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Wagstaff  and  Nguyen  (2002)  on  the  importance  of  health  service  coverage  on  a  child’s  
32:1306:93621:14:14:89:526:281:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:survival.  The  implication  of  this  finding  is  that  if  trade  liberalisation  leads  to  decreased  
32:1307:93728:14:14:89:527:267:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:coverage  of  commune  health  centres,  owing  to  declining  tariff  revenues  and  increased  
32:1308:93825:14:14:89:525:253:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:reliance  on  private  health  services,  then  poor  children’s  health  is  likely  to  be  negatively  
32:1309:93931:14:14:89:137:239:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:affected.  
32:1310:93942:14:13:89:92:225:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
32:1311:93942:13:14:89:161:212:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:7.4 Summary 
32:1312:93954:14:14:89:92:198:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
32:1313:93954:14:14:89:527:184:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:The  results  indicate  the  importance  of  family  background  on  child  health  –  especially  
32:1314:94053:14:13:89:526:170:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:household  assets  and  parental  education  levels  –  and  of  proximity  to  community  public  
32:1315:94152:13:14:89:527:157:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:health  services.  Children’s  involvement  in  work  activities,  although  negative,  did  not  
32:1316:94250:14:0:89:414:143:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:emerge as having a significantly detrimental effect on their health.  
33:1317:94322:0:14:89:316:706:195:g_d0_f7:195:g_d0_f7:C:8. Conclusions and policy challenges   
33:1318:94361:14:13:89:92:692:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
33:1319:94361:13:14:89:526:679:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Although  Vietnam’s  extensive  economic  reforms  –  including  trade  liberalisation  –  over  
33:1320:94458:14:14:89:527:665:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:the  last  two  decades  have  resulted  in  a  significant  reduction  in  national  poverty  rates,  
33:1321:94561:14:14:89:526:651:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:understanding  of  the  differentiated  social  impacts  of  these  reforms  is  still  in  a  fledgling  
33:1322:94667:14:14:89:526:637:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:state.  This  paper  has  sought  to  contribute  to  an  important  dimension  of  this  debate  by  
33:1323:94769:14:13:89:526:623:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:tracing  the  potential  effects  of  trade  liberalisation  on  childhood  poverty.  In  addition  to  
33:1324:94873:13:14:89:526:610:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:individual  child  characteristics  and  several  community-level  infrastructure  variables,  we  
33:1325:94972:14:14:89:528:596:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:have  paid  particular  attention  to  how  household  level  variables  –  including  family  
33:1326:95067:14:14:89:525:582:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:composition, parental education and occupations, gender relations, household wealth and 
33:1327:95155:14:14:89:526:568:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:vulnerability  to  shocks  –  mediate  the  relationship  between  shifts  in  trade  policies  and  
33:1328:95256:14:13:89:201:554:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children’s well-being.  
33:1329:95280:13:14:89:92:541:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
33:1330:95280:14:14:89:525:527:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:While we acknowledge the complexities of tracing the impacts of macro-economic policy 
33:1331:95366:14:14:89:525:513:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:shifts down to the micro-household and intra-household levels, and the limitations of our 
33:1332:95455:14:14:89:526:499:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:sample,  given  that  it  is  not  nationally  representative,33  we  nevertheless  believe  that  this  
33:1333:95560:14:13:89:527:485:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:exercise  serves  to  highlight  some  important  policy  challenges.  In  light  of  Vietnam’s  
33:1334:95657:13:14:89:526:472:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:recent  accession  to  the  WTO  in  November  2006,  we  would  argue  that  it  is  critical  for  
33:1335:95758:14:14:89:526:458:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:policy-makers  and  advocates  for  vulnerable  groups  –  including  children  and  youth  –  to  
33:1336:95857:14:14:89:526:444:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:initiate  a  dialogue  and  to  consider  potential  risks  to  diverse  social  groups.  A  growing  
33:1337:95959:14:14:89:526:430:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:body of international empirical evidence suggests that it will be particularly important to 
33:1338:96051:14:13:89:529:416:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:consider  the  introduction  of  complementary  social  policies  in  order  to  mitigate  the  
33:1339:96147:13:14:89:525:403:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:potentially  adverse  impacts  of  trade  liberalisation  and  to  effectively  harness  the  positive  
33:1340:96251:14:14:89:471:389:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:benefits for as many citizens as possible (eg, Moser, 2003; Veras et al., 2006).  
33:1341:96333:14:14:89:92:375:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
33:1342:96333:14:14:89:528:361:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Overall  our  analysis  suggests  that  children  from  ethnic  minority  group  households,  
33:1343:96427:14:13:89:532:347:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:female-headed   households,   households   with   low   levels   of   maternal   education,   
33:1344:96521:13:14:89:525:334:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:impoverished households that are susceptible to economic shocks, as well as communes 
33:1345:96606:14:14:89:527:320:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:with  a  high  concentration  of  poverty  are  likely  to  be  the  most  vulnerable  to  future  
33:1346:96705:14:14:89:526:306:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:economic reforms and will be most in need of social protection measures. More specific 
33:1347:96791:14:14:89:285:292:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:findings can be summarised as follows:  
33:1348:96831:14:14:89:92:278:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
33:1349:96831:14:13:89:242:264:144:Times:144:Times:C:Ethnic and gender differences 
33:1350:96861:13:14:89:526:251:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Significant  gender  differences  among  children  emerged  only  in  terms  of  girls’  greater  
33:1351:96959:14:14:89:526:237:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:work burden, but it will be important to follow up, to see whether this has a cumulative 
33:1352:97048:14:14:89:525:223:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:impact on their human capital development over time. Ethnicity emerged as an important 
33:1353:97135:14:13:89:527:209:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:variable,  except  in  the  case  of  access  to  private  tuition  (where  wealth  was  the  main  
33:1354:97235:13:14:89:532:196:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:defining   variable).   There   were   significant   differences   in   terms   of   educational   
33:1355:97334:14:14:89:526:182:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:achievement,  with  Kinh  children  performing  better  in  terms  of  reading  and  writing  than  
33:1356:97434:14:14:89:527:168:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:their  ethnic  minority  counterparts.  This  suggests  that  concerted  attention  is  needed  to  
33:1357:97534:14:14:89:528:154:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:address  the  educational  needs  of  children  from  minority  ethnic  groups  especially  as  
33:1358:97630:14:13:89:526:140:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:differences  are  emerging  even  after  just  one  or  two  years  in  school  (among  the  sample  
33:1359:97731:13:14:89:524:127:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:eight-year-old cohort). However, in terms of involvement in child work (domestic chores) 
33:1360:97820:14:14:89:527:113:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and  health  status,  Kinh  (ethnic  majority)  children  fared  worse,  suggesting  that  further  
33:1361:97920:14:14:89:375:99:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:research is needed to understand these surprising findings.  
33:1362:97981:14:0:89:92:85:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
34:1363:97983:0:13:89:244:708:144:Times:144:Times:C:Involvement in work activities  
34:1364:98015:13:14:89:529:695:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Involvement   in   work   (both   chores   and   extra-household   activities)   was   negatively   
34:1365:98115:14:14:89:528:681:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:correlated  with  children’s  access  to  private  tuition,  which  suggests  that  children  are  
34:1366:98214:14:14:89:527:667:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:unlikely  to  benefit  from  the  positive  impact  of  extra  classes  on  children’s  reading  and  
34:1367:98316:14:14:89:527:653:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:writing  (but  not  numeracy)  skills.  It  was  insignificant,  however,  in  terms  of  children’s  
34:1368:98418:14:13:89:526:639:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:health status. This suggests that we need to investigate further how trade liberalisation is 
34:1369:98511:13:14:89:528:626:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:likely  to  affect  children’s  involvement  in  the  labour  market  as  well  as  that  of  their  
34:1370:98612:14:14:89:527:612:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:caregivers,  which  can  have  a  spillover  impact  on  children’s  domestic  and  care  work  
34:1371:98708:14:14:89:128:598:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:burden. 
34:1372:98716:14:14:89:92:584:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
34:1373:98716:14:13:89:278:570:144:Times:144:Times:C:Household poverty and vulnerability   
34:1374:98754:13:14:89:529:557:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:The  household  wealth  index  emerged  as  a  highly  significant  variable  in  terms  of  
34:1375:98847:14:14:89:525:543:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:children’s access to private tuition and educational achievement. Clearly, then, improving 
34:1376:98938:14:14:89:521:529:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:household incomes is important for investments in children’s educational human capital.  
34:1377:99027:14:14:89:526:515:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:However,  household  wealth  was  not  linked  to  children’s  involvement  in  work  activities  
34:1378:99125:14:13:89:526:501:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:(indicating  a  possible  threshold  effect),  nor  to  their  health  status.  Interestingly,  specific  
34:1379:99231:13:14:89:524:488:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:economic shocks did not have a negative impact on children’s well-being, suggesting that 
34:1380:99320:14:14:89:526:474:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:further research is needed to better understand the ways in which households seemingly 
34:1381:99407:14:14:89:527:460:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:protect  their  children  from  the  worst  effects  of  negative  events.  However,  an  overall  
34:1382:99506:14:14:89:529:446:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:decline  in  living  standards  was  positively  correlated  with  an  increase  in  children’s  
34:1383:99603:14:13:89:525:432:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:involvement in work activities as well as weaker numeracy skills. This suggests that we 
34:1384:99691:13:14:89:528:419:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:need  to  better  understand  the  cumulative  impact  of  negative  events  on  household  
34:1385:99783:14:14:89:525:405:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:livelihoods as well as the importance of relative rather than absolute economic downturns 
34:1386:99872:14:14:89:528:391:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:in  order  to  be  able  to  design  more  effective  social  protection  and  social  insurance  
34:1387:99970:14:14:89:158:377:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:mechanisms.  
34:1388:99983:14:13:89:92:363:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B: 
34:1389:99983:13:14:89:191:350:144:Times:144:Times:C:Family composition 
34:1390:100002:14:14:89:526:336:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:The  family  composition  variables  were  mixed,  with  no  clear  patterns  emerging,  except  
34:1391:100099:14:14:89:529:322:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:for   a   greater   work   burden   among   children   in   female-headed   households   and   the   
34:1392:100200:14:13:89:528:308:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:advantage  of  being  a  younger  sibling  in  terms  of  educational  achievement.  Parental  
34:1393:100295:13:14:89:526:295:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:education  had  a  positive  impact  on  children’s  scholastic  achievement  and  health  status,  
34:1394:100395:14:14:89:526:281:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:(and  maternal  education  in  particular  on  reading  and  health),  suggesting  a  link  between  
34:1395:100496:14:14:89:526:267:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:education,  parental  support  and  caring  practices.  This  finding  also  further  reinforces  the  
34:1396:100599:14:14:89:527:253:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:importance  of  investing  in  education,  given  the  possible  intergenerational  impacts  on  
34:1397:100696:14:14:89:176:239:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:child well-being.  
34:1398:100715:14:13:89:92:225:144:Times:144:Times:C: 
34:1399:100715:13:14:89:213:212:144:Times:144:Times:C:Access to public services 
34:1400:100740:14:14:89:525:198:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Access to public services did not affect children’s involvement in work activities, but the 
34:1401:100832:14:14:89:525:184:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:variable emerged as important in terms of children’s educational achievement and health 
34:1402:100920:14:13:89:525:170:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:status. This suggests that if trade liberalisation results in decreased government revenue, 
34:1403:101012:13:14:89:527:157:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and  pro-poor  spending  is  not  adequately  safeguarded,  then  child  well-being  could  be  
34:1404:101108:14:14:89:529:143:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:negatively  affected.  Accordingly,  it  will  be  crucial  to  closely  monitor  government  
34:1405:101202:14:14:89:526:129:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:investment  in  children’s  education  and  health  programmes  post-WTO  accession  and  to  
34:1406:101296:14:14:89:526:115:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:ensure  that  expenditure  trends  match  improved  growth  levels.  Given  that  it  is  expected  
34:1407:101396:14:13:89:527:101:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:that  rapid  privatisation  post-WTO  accession  will  provide  more  opportunities  for  urban  
34:1408:101493:13:0:89:525:88:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and better-off children to get access to good-quality education and health services, it will 
35:1409:101588:0:13:89:526:708:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:be  particularly  important  to  invest  in  improving  public  services  in  poor  and  rural  areas,  
35:1410:101692:13:14:89:526:695:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:which are less likely to benefit from such changes and are already starting from a lower 
35:1411:101780:14:14:89:227:681:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:baseline (eg, Witter, 1996).  
35:1412:101810:14:14:89:92:667:144:Times:144:Times:C: 
35:1413:101810:14:14:89:308:653:144:Times:144:Times:C:Future data collection and research agenda 
35:1414:101853:14:13:89:529:639:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Lastly,  but  perhaps  most  significantly,  our  analysis  highlights  the  need  for  more  
35:1415:101947:13:14:89:528:626:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:comprehensive  data  collection  on  the  multi-dimensionality  of  childhood  poverty  at  
35:1416:102039:14:14:89:530:612:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:different   stages   of   childhood   (early   infancy,   pre-primary   school,   primary   school,   
35:1417:102141:14:14:89:527:598:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:adolescence)  and  on  intra-household  dynamics  –  especially  the  impacts  of  caregivers’  
35:1418:102237:14:14:89:526:584:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:shifting positioning within the labour market – as well as more rigorous analyses of this 
35:1419:102327:14:13:89:525:570:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:data. This will enable the development of social policies that effectively address the often 
35:1420:102420:13:14:89:526:557:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:multiple and overlapping vulnerabilities of children It will be critical for the government 
35:1421:102512:14:14:89:528:543:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:and  donors  to  invest  in  such  research  in  order  to  carry  out  robust  monitoring  and  
35:1422:102609:14:14:89:526:529:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:evaluation  of  the  social  impacts  of  trade  reforms  over  time  so  as  to  better  ensure  that  
35:1423:102713:14:14:89:522:515:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:Vietnam’s  positive  record  of  poverty  alleviation  to  date  is  sustained  and  that  socio-
35:1424:102810:14:13:89:274:501:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:economic inequalities are minimised.
