36:1429:102850:0:14:89:154:708:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:Appendix A 
36:1430:102861:14:14:89:386:694:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: Table 3.1: Summary of Vietnam’s trade reform 
36:1431:102906:14:14:89:92:680:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
36:1432:102906:14:0:89:116:666:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:Date 
36:1433:102911:0:14:140:143:680:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
36:1434:102911:14:14:140:252:666:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C:Trade policy changes 
36:1435:102932:14:14:140:143:652:144:g_d0_f7:144:g_d0_f7:C: 
36:1436:102932:14:15:89:529:638:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:1986 • The  beginning  of  the  economic  reforms,  moving  from  a  centrally  planning  
36:1437:103021:15:14:158:407:623:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:system to a socialist-oriented market-based system. 
36:1438:103073:14:15:89:530:609:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:1987 • A  new  law  on  foreign  investment  introduced  a  remarkably  liberal  regime  
36:1439:103161:15:14:158:388:594:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:for foreign direct investment (FDI) in Vietnam. 
36:1440:103209:14:15:89:529:580:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:1988 • The  Law  on  Export  and  Import  Duties  on  Commercial  Goods  introducing  
36:1441:103294:15:13:158:531:565:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:import  duties,  with  rates  initially  ranging  from  5  to  50  per  cent  became  
36:1442:103380:13:15:158:218:552:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:operational. 
36:1443:103393:15:14:140:532:537:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• Central  government’s  monopoly  of  foreign  trade  was  relaxed,  allowing  
36:1444:103472:14:14:158:530:523:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:licensed  foreign  trading  corporations  and  some  other  firms  to  engage  in  
36:1445:103555:14:14:158:225:509:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:foreign trade. 
36:1446:103570:14:15:89:528:495:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:1990 • A major domestic tax reform was introduced: a special sales tax, a turnover 
36:1447:103651:15:14:158:255:480:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:tax and a profit tax. 
36:1448:103673:14:15:140:378:466:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• Export-import companies required to register 
36:1449:103719:15:14:140:502:451:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• Export of certain commodities limited to relevant exporter associations 
36:1450:103792:14:15:89:535:437:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:1991 • A   regulation   on   setting   up   export   processing   zones   (EPZs)   was   
36:1451:103880:15:15:158:224:422:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:promulgated. 
36:1452:103893:15:14:140:485:407:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• Private companies were allowed to directly engage in foreign trade. 
36:1453:103962:14:14:140:486:393:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• An import duty rebate scheme for export producers was introduced. 
36:1454:104029:14:15:89:531:379:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:1992 • A  trade  agreement  signed  with  the  EU  granted  Vietnam  most-favoured  
36:1455:104112:15:14:158:529:364:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:nation  (MFN)  treatment  in  EU  markets,  established  quotas  for  exports  of  
36:1456:104195:14:14:158:531:350:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:textiles  and  clothing  to  EU  and  granted  tariff  preferences  on  selected  
36:1457:104277:14:14:158:320:336:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:imports to Vietnam from the EU. 
36:1458:104309:14:15:140:488:322:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• The harmonised system (HS) of tariff nomenclature was introduced. 
36:1459:104376:15:14:89:528:307:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:1993 • Export shipment licensing was relaxed, with six-month licences (in place of 
36:1460:104458:14:15:158:503:293:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:shipment-by-shipment licences) introduced for 22 export commodities. 
36:1461:104527:15:15:140:329:278:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• Custom declaration form improved 
36:1462:104561:15:14:140:302:263:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• Duty rebate system improved 
36:1463:104590:14:15:89:530:249:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:1994 • Import  permits  were  abolished  for  all  but  15  products.  Export  shipment  
36:1464:104678:15:14:158:519:234:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:licensing was abolished for all products except rice, timber and petroleum. 
36:1465:104754:14:15:140:307:220:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• GATT observer status granted 
36:1466:104784:15:15:89:441:205:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:1995 • Export quotas were eliminated on all products except rice. 
36:1467:104849:15:14:140:529:190:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• Shipment-by-shipment  licensing  requirement  was  lifted  from  a  wide  range  
36:1468:104931:14:15:158:321:176:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:of consumer and producer goods. 
36:1469:104963:15:14:140:504:161:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• The number of products subject to import quotas was reduced to seven. 
36:1470:105034:14:14:140:533:147:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• Vietnam  became  a  member  of  ASEAN  and  acceded  to  protocols  of  
36:1471:105107:14:15:158:421:133:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:membership of the ASEAN Free Trade Area (AFTA). 
36:1472:105155:15:14:140:353:118:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• Vietnam applied for WTO membership. 
36:1473:105192:14:15:140:329:104:144:g_d0_f13:144:g_d0_f6:A:• Export tariff raised for 11 products 
36:1474:105230:15:0:89:530:89:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:B:1996 • A  new  law  on  foreign  investment  reduced  the  coverage  of  import  duty  
37:1475:105318:0:15:158:371:708:144:g_d0_f6:144:g_d0_f6:A:exemptions for foreign investment projects.

58:2434:167920:7:16:90:521:547:42:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:2 Over the last decade Vietnam has averaged a 7 per cent per annum growth rate. The poverty rate declined 
58:2435:168026:16:12:89:523:531:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:from 58 per cent in 1993 to 24.1 per cent in 2004 (Achieving the Millennium Development Goals, Report of 
58:2436:168130:12:21:89:160:519:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:Vietnam, 2005).  
58:2437:168147:21:16:90:488:498:42:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:3 Senapaty (2003) argues that the relationship between gender and trade liberalisation is a two-way 
58:2438:168246:16:11:89:514:482:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:relationship: (i) trade liberalisation brings different costs and benefits to men and women, and this gender 
58:2439:168355:11:12:89:522:471:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:bias cuts across all economic and social categories; and (ii) the impact of trade liberalisation is mediated by 
58:2440:168467:12:11:89:502:459:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:gender relations and gendered social, economic and political structures. These structures may be in the 
58:2441:168571:11:12:89:503:448:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:form of gender gaps in education and health; patterns of labour market discrimination and labour force 
58:2442:168673:12:21:89:470:436:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:participation levels; gendered patterns of rights and resources; and other socio-cultural factors. 
58:2443:168772:21:16:90:512:415:42:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:4 Ideally we should also pay attention to the potential impacts of trade liberalisation on women in light of 
58:2444:168881:16:11:89:520:399:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:their role as the primary caregivers in the large majority of Vietnamese households (Tuan et al., 2003). We 
58:2445:168989:11:12:89:505:388:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:would hypothesise that changes in women’s access to labour markets and their time allocation between 
58:2446:169090:12:11:89:516:376:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:productive and social reproductive activities are likely to have an important spillover impact on child well-
58:2447:169199:11:21:89:431:365:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:being. However, data limitations preclude us from exploring this route in any depth.  
58:2448:169285:21:16:90:477:344:42:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:5 The 2006 World Development Report found that 0–14 year olds comprised 30.3 per cent of the 
58:2449:169378:16:12:90:517:328:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:Vietnamese population. If we were also to include 15–17-year-olds in line with the UN Convention on the 
58:2450:169482:12:11:90:521:316:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:Rights of the Child 1989 (UNCRC) definition of children (people under 18 years of age), the figures would 
58:2451:169588:11:21:90:236:305:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:be higher still (World Bank, 2006).  
58:2452:169625:21:16:90:309:284:42:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:6 See www.younglives.org.uk for further information.  
58:2453:169678:16:7:90:93:268:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F: 
58:2454:169678:7:16:90:509:261:42:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:7 Winters et al.  (2002) argue that both trade liberalisation and poverty are not easily measured and trade 
58:2455:169786:16:12:90:382:245:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:liberalisation takes place in tandem with other macro-economic reforms. 
58:2456:169858:12:7:90:93:233:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F: 
58:2457:169858:7:16:90:411:226:42:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:8 Analyses of the gendered dimensions of trade have highlighted the following:  
58:2458:169938:16:11:108:511:210:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:a) although trade liberalisation often results in better earning opportunities for women – especially 
58:2459:170039:11:12:126:515:199:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:factory jobs in export-oriented sectors, as exemplified by the maquilladora sector in Mexico and 
58:2460:170136:12:11:126:502:187:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:women’s entry into export-free-zones in East Asia – these jobs tend to be at the bottom of the 
58:2461:170231:11:12:126:368:176:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:international labour chain and are often highly exploitative;  
58:2462:170294:12:11:108:496:164:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:b) owing in part to women’s domestic responsibilities (and pressures to enter and exit from the 
58:2463:170389:11:12:126:524:153:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:labour market more frequently) as well as lower investment in female education and human capital 
58:2464:170486:12:11:126:516:141:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:in many developing countries, women tend to have unequal access to labour markets, which puts 
58:2465:170580:11:12:126:508:130:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:them at a disadvantage in the context of liberalisation. This includes women’s disproportionate 
58:2466:170676:12:11:126:518:118:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:positioning in the informal sector, further excluding them from the benefits of new labour market 
58:2467:170774:11:12:126:276:107:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:opportunities (eg, Sweetman, 2004).  
58:2468:170811:12:0:108:111:95:100:g_d0_f6:100:g_d0_f6:F:
